class="docMainContainer_a9sJ"><div class="container padding-top--md padding-bottom--lg"><div class="row"><div class="col docItemCol_Qr34"><div class="docItemContainer_tjFy"><article><nav class="theme-doc-breadcrumbs breadcrumbsContainer_T5ub" aria-label="Breadcrumbs"><ul class="breadcrumbs"><li class="breadcrumbs__item"><a aria-label="Home page" class="breadcrumbs__link" href="/"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="breadcrumbHomeIcon_sfvy"><path d="M10 19v-5h4v5c0 .55.45 1 1 1h3c.55 0 1-.45 1-1v-7h1.7c.46 0 .68-.57.33-.87L12.67 3.6c-.38-.34-.96-.34-1.34 0l-8.36 7.53c-.34.3-.13.87.33.87H5v7c0 .55.45 1 1 1h3c.55 0 1-.45 1-1z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a></li><li class="breadcrumbs__item"><a class="breadcrumbs__link" href="/docs/providers/"><span>Providers</span></a></li><li class="breadcrumbs__item breadcrumbs__item--active"><span class="breadcrumbs__link">OpenAI</span></li></ul></nav><div class="tocCollapsible_wXna theme-doc-toc-mobile tocMobile_Ojys"><button type="button" class="clean-btn tocCollapsibleButton_iI2p">On this page</button></div><div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><div style="position:relative"><header><h1>OpenAI</h1></header>
<p>To use the OpenAI API, set the <code>OPENAI_API_KEY</code> environment variable, specify via <code>apiKey</code> field in the configuration file or pass the API key as an argument to the constructor.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-sh codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-sh codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token builtin class-name">export</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token assign-left variable" style="color:#36acaa">OPENAI_API_KEY</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token plain">your_api_key_here</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The OpenAI provider supports the following model formats:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>openai:chat:&lt;model name&gt;</code> - uses any model name against the <code>/v1/chat/completions</code> endpoint</li>
<li class=""><code>openai:responses:&lt;model name&gt;</code> - uses responses API models over HTTP connections</li>
<li class=""><code>openai:assistant:&lt;assistant id&gt;</code> - use an assistant</li>
<li class=""><code>openai:&lt;model name&gt;</code> - uses a specific model name (mapped automatically to chat or completion endpoint)</li>
<li class=""><code>openai:chat</code> - defaults to <code>gpt-5-mini</code></li>
<li class=""><code>openai:chat:ft:gpt-5-mini:company-name:ID</code> - example of a fine-tuned chat completion model</li>
<li class=""><code>openai:completion</code> - defaults to <code>text-davinci-003</code></li>
<li class=""><code>openai:completion:&lt;model name&gt;</code> - uses any model name against the <code>/v1/completions</code> endpoint</li>
<li class=""><code>openai:embeddings:&lt;model name&gt;</code> - uses any model name against the <code>/v1/embeddings</code> endpoint</li>
<li class=""><code>openai:realtime:&lt;model name&gt;</code> - uses realtime API models over WebSocket connections</li>
</ul>
<p>The <code>openai:&lt;endpoint&gt;:&lt;model name&gt;</code> construction is useful if OpenAI releases a new model,
or if you have a custom model.
For example, if OpenAI releases <code>gpt-5</code> chat completion,
you could begin using it immediately with <code>openai:chat:gpt-5</code>.</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">GPT-5 only: verbosity and minimal reasoning</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">effort</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> minimal</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The OpenAI provider supports a handful of <a href="https://github.com/promptfoo/promptfoo/blob/main/src/providers/openai/types.ts#L112-L185" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">configuration options</a>, such as <code>temperature</code>, <code>functions</code>, and <code>tools</code>, which can be used to customize the behavior of the model like so:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> openai</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">gpt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">5</span><span class="token <blockquote>
<p><strong>Note:</strong> OpenAI models can also be accessed through <a class="" href="/docs/providers/azure/">Azure OpenAI</a>, which offers additional enterprise features, compliance options, and regional availability.</p>
</blockquote>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="formatting-chat-messages">Formatting chat messages<a href="#formatting-chat-messages" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Formatting chat messages" title="Direct link to Formatting chat messages" translate="no"></a></h2>
<p>For information on setting up chat conversation, see <a class="" href="/docs/configuration/chat/">chat threads</a>.</p>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="configuring-parameters">Configuring parameters<a href="#configuring-parameters" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Configuring parameters" title="Direct link to Configuring parameters" translate="no"></a></h2>
<p>The <code>providers</code> list takes a <code>config</code> key that allows you to set parameters like <code>temperature</code>, <code>max_tokens</code>, and <a href="https://platform.openai.com/docs/api-reference/chat/create#chat/create-temperature" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">others</a>. For example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> openai</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">gpt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">5</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">mini</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">temperature</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">128</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">apiKey</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> sk</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">abc123</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Supported parameters include:</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>apiBaseUrl</code></td><td>The base URL of the OpenAI API, please also read <code>OPENAI_BASE_URL</code> below.</td></tr><tr><td><code>apiHost</code></td><td>The hostname of the OpenAI API, please also read <code>OPENAI_API_HOST</code> below.</td></tr><tr><td><code>apiKey</code></td><td>Your OpenAI API key, equivalent to <code>OPENAI_API_KEY</code> environment variable</td></tr><tr><td><code>apiKeyEnvar</code></td><td>An environment variable that contains the API key</td></tr><tr><td><code>best_of</code></td><td>Controls the number of alternative outputs to generate and select from.</td></tr><tr><td><code>frequency_penalty</code></td><td>Applies a penalty to frequent tokens, making them less likely to appear in the output.</td></tr><tr><td><code>function_call</code></td><td>Controls whether the AI should call functions. Can be either &#x27;none&#x27;, &#x27;auto&#x27;, or an object with a <code>name</code> that specifies the function to call.</td></tr><tr><td><code>functions</code></td><td>Allows you to define custom functions. Each function should be an object with a <code>name</code>, optional <code>description</code>, and <code>parameters</code>.</td></tr><tr><td><code>functionToolCallbacks</code></td><td>A map of function tool names to function callbacks. Each callback should accept a string and return a string or a <code>Promise&lt;string&gt;</code>.</td></tr><tr><td><code>headers</code></td><td>Additional headers to include in the request.</td></tr><tr><td><code>max_tokens</code></td><td>Controls the maximum length of the output in tokens. Not valid for reasoning models (o1, o3, o3-pro, o3-mini, o4-mini).</td></tr><tr><td><code>maxRetries</code></td><td>Maximum number of retry attempts for failed API requests. Defaults to 4. Set to 0 to disable retries.</td></tr><tr><td><code>metadata</code></td><td>Key-value pairs for request tagging and organization.</td></tr><tr><td><code>organization</code></td><td>Your OpenAI organization key.</td></tr><tr><td><code>passthrough</code></td><td>A flexible object that allows passing arbitrary parameters directly to the OpenAI API request body. Useful for experimental, new, or provider-specific parameters not yet explicitly supported in promptfoo. This parameter is merged into the final API request and can override other settings.</td></tr><tr><td><code>presence_penalty</code></td><td>Applies a penalty to new tokens (tokens that haven&#x27;t appeared in the input), making them less likely to appear in the output.</td></tr><tr><td><code>reasoning</code></td><td>Enhanced reasoning configuration for o-series models. Object with <code>effort</code> (&#x27;low&#x27;, &#x27;medium&#x27;, &#x27;high&#x27;) and optional <code>summary</code> (&#x27;auto&#x27;, &#x27;concise&#x27;, &#x27;detailed&#x27;) fields.</td></tr><tr><td><code>response_format</code></td><td>Specifies the desired output format, including <code>json_object</code> and <code>json_schema</code>. Can also be specified in the prompt config. If specified in both, the prompt config takes precedence.</td></tr><tr><td><code>seed</code></td><td>Seed used for deterministic output.</td></tr><tr><td><code>stop</code></td><td>Defines a list of tokens that signal the end of the output.</td></tr><tr><td><code>store</code></td><td>Whether to store the conversation for future retrieval (boolean).</td></tr><tr><td><code>temperature</code></td><td>Controls the randomness of the AI&#x27;s output. Higher values (close to 1) make the output more random, while lower values (close to 0) make it more deterministic.</td></tr><tr><td><code>tool_choice</code></td><td>Controls whether the AI should use a tool. See <a href="https://platform.openai.com/docs/api-reference/chat/create#chat-create-tools" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">OpenAI Tools documentation</a></td></tr><tr><td><code>tools</code></td><td>Allows you to define custom tools. See <a href="https://platform.openai.com/docs/api-reference/chat/create#chat-create-tools" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">OpenAI Tools documentation</a></td></tr><tr><td><code>top_p</code></td><td>Controls the nucleus sampling, a method that helps control the randomness of the AI&#x27;s output.</td></tr><tr><td><code>user</code></td><td>A unique identifier representing your end-user, for tracking and abuse prevention.</td></tr><tr><td><code>max_completion_tokens</code></td><td>Maximum number of tokens to generate for reasoning models (o1, o3, o3-pro, o3-mini, o4-mini).</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>Here are the type declarations of <code>config</code> parameters:</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="models">Models<a href="#models" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Models" title="Direct link to Models" translate="no"></a></h2>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="gpt-41">GPT-4.1<a href="#gpt-41" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to GPT-4.1" title="Direct link to GPT-4.1" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>GPT-4.1 is OpenAI&#x27;s flagship model for complex tasks with a 1,047,576 token context window and 32,768 max output tokens. Available in three variants with different price points:</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>Model</th><th>Description</th><th>Input Price</th><th>Output Price</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>GPT-4.1</td><td>Flagship model for complex tasks</td><td>$2.00 per 1M tokens</td><td>$8.00 per 1M tokens</td></tr><tr><td>GPT-4.1 Mini</td><td>More affordable, strong general capabilities</td><td>$0.40 per 1M tokens</td><td>$1.60 per 1M tokens</td></tr><tr><td>GPT-4.1 Nano</td><td>Most economical, good for high-volume tasks</td><td>$0.10 per 1M tokens</td><td>$0.40 per 1M tokens</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>All variants support text and image input with text output and have a May 31, 2024 knowledge cutoff.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="usage-examples">Usage Examples<a href="#usage-examples" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Usage Examples" title="Direct link to Usage Examples" translate="no"></a></h4>
<p>Standard model:</p>

<p>More affordable variants:</p>

<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="gpt-51">GPT-5.1<a href="#gpt-51" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to GPT-5.1" title="Direct link to GPT-5.1" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>GPT-5.1 is OpenAI&#x27;s newest flagship model, part of the GPT-5 model family. It excels at coding and agentic tasks with improved steerability, a new <code>none</code> reasoning mode for faster responses, and new tools for coding use cases.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="available-models">Available Models<a href="#available-models" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Available Models" title="Direct link to Available Models" translate="no"></a></h4>
<table><thead><tr><th>Model</th><th>Description</th><th>Best For</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>gpt-5.1</td><td>Latest flagship model</td><td>Complex reasoning and broad world knowledge</td></tr><tr><td>gpt-5.1-2025-11-13</td><td>Dated snapshot version</td><td>Locked behavior for production</td></tr><tr><td>gpt-5.1-mini</td><td>Cost-optimized reasoning</td><td>Balanced speed, cost, and capability</td></tr><tr><td>gpt-5.1-nano</td><td>High-throughput model</td><td>Simple instruction-following tasks</td></tr><tr><td>gpt-5.1-codex</td><td>Specialized for coding tasks in Codex environments</td><td>Agentic coding workflows</td></tr><tr><td>gpt-5.1-codex-max</td><td>Frontier agentic coding model with compaction</td><td>Long-running coding tasks and refactors</td></tr><tr><td>gpt-5.1-chat-latest</td><td>Chat-optimized alias</td><td>Conversational applications</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="key-features">Key Features<a href="#key-features" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Key Features" title="Direct link to Key Features" translate="no"></a></h4>
<p>GPT-5.1 introduces several improvements over GPT-5:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong><code>none</code> reasoning mode</strong>: New lowest reasoning setting for low-latency interactions (default setting)</li>
<li class=""><strong>Increased steerability</strong>: Better control over personality, tone, and output format</li>
<li class=""><strong>Configurable verbosity</strong>: Control output length with <code>low</code>, <code>medium</code>, or <code>high</code> settings (default: <code>medium</code>)</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="usage-examples-1">Usage Examples<a href="#usage-examples-1" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Usage Examples" title="Direct link to Usage Examples" translate="no"></a></h4>

style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;high&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Maximum reasoning for complex tasks</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">verbosity</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;medium&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Balanced output length</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_output_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">4096</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="reasoning-modes">Reasoning Modes<a href="#reasoning-modes" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Reasoning Modes" title="Direct link to Reasoning Modes" translate="no"></a></h4>
<p>GPT-5.1 supports four reasoning effort levels:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong><code>none</code></strong> (default): No reasoning tokens, fastest responses, similar to non-reasoning models</li>
<li class=""><strong><code>low</code></strong>: Minimal reasoning for straightforward tasks</li>
<li class=""><strong><code>medium</code></strong>: Balanced reasoning for moderate complexity</li>
<li class=""><strong><code>high</code></strong>: Maximum reasoning for complex problem-solving</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="migration-from-gpt-5">Migration from GPT-5<a href="#migration-from-gpt-5" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Migration from GPT-5" title="Direct link to Migration from GPT-5" translate="no"></a></h4>
<p>GPT-5.1 with default settings (<code>none</code> reasoning) is designed as a drop-in replacement for GPT-5. Key differences:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">GPT-5.1 defaults to <code>none</code> reasoning effort (GPT-5 defaulted to <code>low</code>)</li>
<li class="">GPT-5.1 has better-calibrated reasoning token consumption</li>
<li class="">Improved instruction-following and output formatting</li>
</ul>
<p>For tasks requiring reasoning, start with <code>medium</code> effort and increase to <code>high</code> if needed.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="gpt-51-codex-max">GPT-5.1-Codex-Max<a href="#gpt-51-codex-max" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to GPT-5.1-Codex-Max" title="Direct link to GPT-5.1-Codex-Max" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>GPT-5.1-Codex-Max is OpenAI&#x27;s frontier agentic coding model, built on an updated foundational reasoning model trained on agentic tasks across software engineering, math, research, and more. It&#x27;s designed for long-running, detailed coding work.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="key-capabilities">Key Capabilities<a href="#key-capabilities" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Key Capabilities" title="Direct link to Key Capabilities" translate="no"></a></h4>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Compaction</strong>: First model natively trained to operate across multiple context windows through compaction, coherently working over millions of tokens in a single task</li>
<li class=""><strong>Long-running tasks</strong>: Supports project-scale refactors, deep debugging sessions, and multi-hour agent loops</li>
<li class=""><strong>Token efficiency</strong>: 30% fewer thinking tokens compared to GPT-5.1-Codex at the same reasoning effort level</li>
<li class=""><strong>Windows support</strong>: First model trained to operate in Windows environments</li>
<li class=""><strong>Improved collaboration</strong>: Better performance as a coding partner in CLI environments</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="usage-examples-2">Usage Examples<a href="#usage-examples-2" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Usage Examples" title="Direct link to Usage Examples" translate="no"></a></h4>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div <p>For latency-insensitive tasks requiring maximum quality:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div <div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-warning admonition_WCGJ alert alert--warning"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8.893 1.5c-.183-.31-.52-.5-.887-.5s-.703.19-.886.5L.138 13.499a.98.98 0 0 0 0 1.001c.193.31.53.501.886.501h13.964c.367 0 .704-.19.877-.5a1.03 1.03 0 0 0 .01-1.002L8.893 1.5zm.133 11.497H6.987v-2.003h2.039v2.003zm0-3.004H6.987V5.987h2.039v4.006z"></path></svg></span>warning</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>GPT-5.1-Codex-Max is only available through the Responses API (<code>openai:responses:</code>). <h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="reasoning-effort-levels">Reasoning Effort Levels<a href="#reasoning-effort-levels" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Reasoning Effort Levels" title="Direct link to Reasoning Effort Levels" translate="no"></a></h4>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong><code>low</code></strong>: Minimal reasoning for straightforward tasks</li>
<li class=""><strong><code>medium</code></strong>: Balanced reasoning, recommended as daily driver</li>
<li class=""><strong><code>high</code></strong>: Maximum reasoning for complex problem-solving</li>
<li class=""><strong><code>xhigh</code></strong>: Extra high reasoning for non-latency-sensitive tasks requiring best results</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="best-practices">Best Practices<a href="#best-practices" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Best Practices" title="Direct link to Best Practices" translate="no"></a></h4>
<ul>
<li class="">Use for agentic coding tasks in Codex or Codex-like environments</li>
<li class="">Reserve at least 25,000 tokens for reasoning and outputs when starting</li>
<li class="">Start with <code>medium</code> reasoning effort for most tasks</li>
<li class="">Use <code>xhigh</code> effort only for complex tasks where latency is not a concern</li>
<li class="">Review agent work before deploying to production</li>
</ul>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-note admonition_WCGJ alert alert--secondary"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.3 5.69a.942.942 0 0 1-.28-.7c0-.28.09-.52.28-.7.19-.18.42-.28.7-.28.28 0 .52.09.7.28.18.19.28.42.28.7 0 .28-.09.52-.28.7a1 1 0 0 1-.7.3c-.28 0-.52-.11-.7-.3zM8 7.99c-.02-.25-.11-.48-.31-.69-.2-.19-.42-.3-.69-.31H6c-.27.02-.48.13-.69.31-.2.2-.3.44-.31.69h1v3c.02.27.11.5.31.69.2.2.42.31.69.31h1c.27 0 .48-.11.69-.31.2-.19.3-.42.31-.69H8V7.98v.01zM7 2.3c-3.14 0-5.7 2.54-5.7 5.68 0 3.14 2.56 5.7 5.7 5.7s5.7-2.55 5.7-5.7c0-3.15-2.56-5.69-5.7-5.69v.01zM7 .98c3.86 0 7 3.14 7 7s-3.14 7-7 7-7-3.12-7-7 3.14-7 7-7z"></path></svg></span>note</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>GPT-5.1-Codex-Max is recommended for use only in agentic coding environments and is not a general-purpose model like GPT-5.1.</p></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="gpt-52">GPT-5.2<a href="#gpt-52" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to GPT-5.2" title="Direct link to GPT-5.2" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>GPT-5.2 is OpenAI&#x27;s flagship model for coding and agentic tasks. It offers significant improvements in safety, instruction following, and reduced deception compared to GPT-5.1.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="available-models-1">Available Models<a href="#available-models-1" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Available Models" title="Direct link to Available Models" translate="no"></a></h4>
<table><thead><tr><th>Model</th><th>Description</th><th>Best For</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>gpt-5.2</td><td>Flagship model for coding and agentic</td><td>Complex reasoning and coding tasks</td></tr><tr><td>gpt-5.2-2025-12-11</td><td>Snapshot version</td><td>Locked behavior for production</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="key-specifications">Key Specifications<a href="#key-specifications" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Key Specifications" title="Direct link to Key Specifications" translate="no"></a></h4>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Context window</strong>: 400,000 tokens</li>
<li class=""><strong>Max output tokens</strong>: 128,000 tokens</li>
<li class=""><strong>Reasoning support</strong>: Full reasoning token support with configurable effort levels</li>
<li class=""><strong>Pricing</strong>: $1.75 per 1M input tokens, $14 per 1M output tokens</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="usage-examples-3">Usage Examples<a href="#usage-examples-3" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Usage Examples" title="Direct link to Usage Examples" translate="no"></a></h4>

<p><strong>Chat Completions API:</strong></p>

<p>Fast, low-latency responses (no reasoning):</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">5.2</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">reasoning_effort</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;none&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_completion_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">2048</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Responses API</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> openai</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">responses</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">gpt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">5.2</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">reasoning</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">effort</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;none&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_output_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">2048</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="key-improvements-over-gpt-51">Key Improvements over GPT-5.1<a href="#key-improvements-over-gpt-51" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Key Improvements over GPT-5.1" title="Direct link to Key Improvements over GPT-5.1" translate="no"></a></h4>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Reduced deception</strong>: Significantly lower deception rates in production traffic</li>
<li class=""><strong>Better safety compliance</strong>: Improved cyber safety policy compliance</li>
<li class=""><strong>Improved prompt injection resistance</strong>: Enhanced robustness to known prompt injection attacks</li>
<li class=""><strong>Enhanced sensitive topic handling</strong>: Better performance on mental health and emotional reliance evaluations</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="reasoning-effort-levels-1">Reasoning Effort Levels<a href="#reasoning-effort-levels-1" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Reasoning Effort Levels" title="Direct link to Reasoning Effort Levels" translate="no"></a></h4>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong><code>none</code></strong>: No reasoning tokens, fastest responses</li>
<li class=""><strong><code>low</code></strong>: Minimal reasoning for straightforward tasks</li>
<li class=""><strong><code>medium</code></strong>: Balanced reasoning for moderate complexity</li>
<li class=""><strong><code>high</code></strong>: Maximum reasoning for complex problem-solving</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="reasoning-models-o1-o3-o3-pro-o3-mini-o4-mini">Reasoning Models (o1, o3, o3-pro, o3-mini, o4-mini)<a href="#reasoning-models-o1-o3-o3-pro-o3-mini-o4-mini" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Reasoning Models (o1, o3, o3-pro, o3-mini, o4-mini)" title="Direct link to Reasoning Models (o1, o3, o3-pro, o3-mini, o4-mini)" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>Reasoning models, like <code>o1</code>, <code>o3</code>, <code>o3-pro</code>, <code>o3-mini</code>, and <code>o4-mini</code>, are large language models trained with reinforcement learning to perform complex reasoning. These models excel in complex problem-solving, coding, scientific reasoning, and multi-step planning for agentic workflows.</p>
<p>When using reasoning models, there are important differences in how tokens are handled:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> openai</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">o1</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">reasoning</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">effort</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;medium&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Can be &quot;low&quot;, &quot;medium&quot;, or &quot;high&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_completion_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">25000</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Can also be set via OPENAI_MAX_COMPLETION_TOKENS env var</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Unlike standard models that use <code>max_tokens</code>, reasoning models use:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>max_completion_tokens</code> to control the total tokens generated (both reasoning and visible output)</li>
<li class=""><code>reasoning</code> to control how thoroughly the model thinks before responding (with <code>effort</code>: none (GPT-5.1 only), low, medium, high)</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="how-reasoning-models-work">How Reasoning Models Work<a href="#how-reasoning-models-work" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to How Reasoning Models Work" title="Direct link to How Reasoning Models Work" translate="no"></a></h4>
<p>Reasoning models &quot;think before they answer,&quot; generating internal reasoning tokens that:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Are not visible in the output</li>
<li class="">Count towards token usage and billing</li>
<li class="">Occupy space in the context window</li>
</ul>
<p>Both <code>o1</code> and <code>o3-mini</code> models have a 128,000 token context window, while <code>o3-pro</code> and <code>o4-mini</code> have a 200,000 token context window. OpenAI recommends reserving at least 25,000 tokens for reasoning and outputs when starting with these models.</p>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="images">Images<a href="#images" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Images" title="Direct link to Images" translate="no"></a></h2>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="sending-images-in-prompts">Sending images in prompts<a href="#sending-images-in-prompts" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Sending images in prompts" title="Direct link to Sending images in prompts" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>You can include images in the prompt by using content blocks. For example, here&#x27;s an example config:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div <h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="generating-images">Generating images<a href="#generating-images" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Generating images" title="Direct link to Generating images" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>OpenAI supports image generation via <code>openai:image:&lt;model&gt;</code>. Supported models include:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>gpt-image-1.5</code> - OpenAI&#x27;s state-of-the-art image generation model with best instruction following</li>
<li class=""><code>gpt-image-1</code> - High-quality image generation model</li>
<li class=""><code>gpt-image-1-mini</code> - Cost-efficient version of GPT Image 1</li>
<li class=""><code>dall-e-3</code> - High quality image generation with larger resolution support</li>
<li class=""><code>dall-e-2</code> - Lower cost option with concurrent requests support</li>
</ul>
<p>See the <a href="https://github.com/promptfoo/promptfoo/tree/main/examples/openai-images" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">OpenAI image generation example</a>.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="gpt-image-15">GPT Image 1.5<a href="#gpt-image-15" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to GPT Image 1.5" title="Direct link to GPT Image 1.5" translate="no"></a></h4>
<p>GPT Image 1.5 is OpenAI&#x27;s most advanced image generation model with superior instruction following, prompt adherence, and photorealistic quality. It uses token-based pricing for more flexible cost control.</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> openai</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">image</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">gpt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">image</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">1.5</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">size</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> 1024x1024 </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># 1024x1024, 1024x1536, 1536x1024, or auto</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">quality</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> low </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># low, medium, high, or auto</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">background</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> transparent </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># transparent, opaque, or auto</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">output_format</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> png </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># png, jpeg, or webp</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">output_compression</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">80</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># 0-100, only for jpeg/webp</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">moderation</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> auto </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># auto or low</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<table><thead><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th><th>Options</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>size</code></td><td>Image dimensions</td><td><code>1024x1024</code>, <code>1024x1536</code>, <code>1536x1024</code>, <code>auto</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>quality</code></td><td>Rendering quality</td><td><code>low</code>, <code>medium</code>, <code>high</code>, <code>auto</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>background</code></td><td>Background transparency (png/webp only)</td><td><code>transparent</code>, <code>opaque</code>, <code>auto</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>output_format</code></td><td>Output image format</td><td><code>png</code>, <code>jpeg</code>, <code>webp</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>output_compression</code></td><td>Compression level (jpeg/webp only)</td><td><code>0-100</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>moderation</code></td><td>Content moderation strictness</td><td><code>auto</code>, <code>low</code></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><strong>Pricing:</strong></p>
<p>GPT Image 1.5 uses token-based pricing at $5/1M input text tokens, $10/1M output text tokens, $8/1M input image tokens, and $32/1M output image tokens. Estimated costs per image:</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>Quality</th><th>1024x1024</th><th>1024x1536</th><th>1536x1024</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Low</td><td>~$0.064</td><td>~$0.096</td><td>~$0.096</td></tr><tr><td>Medium</td><td>~$0.128</td><td>~$0.192</td><td>~$0.192</td></tr><tr><td>High</td><td>~$0.192</td><td>~$0.288</td><td>~$0.288</td></tr></tbody></table>

<p>To display images in the web viewer, wrap vars or outputs in markdown image tags like so:</p>
<div class="language-markdown codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-markdown codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">![](/path/to/myimage.png)</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Then, enable &#x27;Render markdown&#x27; under Table Settings.</p>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="web-search-support">Web Search Support<a href="#web-search-support" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Web Search Support" title="Direct link to Web Search Support" translate="no"></a></h2>
<p>The OpenAI Responses API supports web search capabilities through the <code>web_search_preview</code> tool, which enables the <code>search-rubric</code> assertion type. This allows models to search the web for current information and verify facts.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="enabling-web-search">Enabling Web Search<a href="#enabling-web-search" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Enabling Web Search" title="Direct link to Enabling Web Search" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>To enable web search with the OpenAI Responses API, use the <code>openai:responses</code> provider format and add the <code>web_search_preview</code> tool to your configuration:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> openai</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">responses</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">gpt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">5.1</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tools</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> web_search_preview</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="using-web-search-assertions">Using Web Search Assertions<a href="#using-web-search-assertions" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Using Web Search Assertions" title="Direct link to Using Web Search Assertions" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>The <code>search-rubric</code> assertion type uses web search to quickly verify current information:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Real-time data (weather, stock prices, news)</li>
<li class="">Current events and statistics</li>
<li class="">Time-sensitive information</li>
<li class="">Quick fact verification</li>
</ul>
<p>Example configuration:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span City</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="cost-considerations">Cost Considerations<a href="#cost-considerations" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Cost Considerations" title="Direct link to Cost Considerations" translate="no"></a></h3>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_WCGJ alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>info</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>Web search calls in the Responses API are billed separately from normal tokens:</p><ul>
<li class="">The web search tool costs <strong>$10 per 1,000 calls</strong> for the standard tool and <strong>$10-25 per 1,000 calls</strong> for preview variants, plus any search content tokens where applicable</li>
<li class="">Each search-rubric assertion may perform one or more searches</li>
<li class="">Caching is enabled by default; use <code>--no-cache</code> to force fresh searches during development</li>
<li class="">See <a href="https://openai.com/api/pricing/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">OpenAI&#x27;s pricing page</a> for current rates</li>
</ul></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="best-practices-1">Best Practices<a href="#best-practices-1" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Best Practices" title="Direct link to Best Practices" translate="no"></a></h3>
<ol>
<li class=""><strong>Use specific search queries</strong>: More specific queries yield better verification results</li>
<li class=""><strong>Use caching</strong>: Caching is enabled by default; results are reused to avoid repeated searches</li>
<li class=""><strong>Use appropriate models</strong>: gpt-5.1-mini is recommended for cost-effective web search</li>
<li class=""><strong>Monitor usage</strong>: Track API costs, especially in CI/CD pipelines</li>
</ol>
<p>For more details on using search-rubric assertions, see the <a class="" href="/docs/configuration/expected-outputs/model-graded/search-rubric/">Search-Rubric documentation</a>.</p>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="using-tools-and-functions">Using tools and functions<a href="#using-tools-and-functions" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Using tools and functions" title="Direct link to Using tools and functions" translate="no"></a></h2>
<p>OpenAI tools and functions are supported. See <a href="https://github.com/promptfoo/promptfoo/tree/main/examples/openai-tools-call" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">OpenAI tools example</a> and <a href="https://github.com/promptfoo/promptfoo/tree/main/examples/openai-function-call" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">OpenAI functions example</a>.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="using-tools">Using tools<a href="#using-tools" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Using tools" title="Direct link to Using tools" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>To set <code>tools</code> on an OpenAI provider, use the provider&#x27;s <code>config</code> key. The model may return tool calls in two formats:</p>
<ol>
<li class="">An array of tool calls: <code>[{type: &#x27;function&#x27;, function: {...}}]</code></li>
<li class="">A message with tool calls: <code>{content: &#x27;...&#x27;, tool_calls: [{type: &#x27;function&#x27;, function: {...}}]}</code></li>
</ol>
<p>Tools can be defined inline or loaded from an external file:</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_WCGJ alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Supported file formats</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>Tools can be loaded from external files in multiple formats:</p><div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tools</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> file</span><span class="token punctuation" The function can be synchronous or asynchronous.</p><p><strong>Asynchronous example:</strong></p><div class="language-javascript codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" <p>Sometimes OpenAI function calls don&#x27;t match <code>tools</code> schemas. Use <a class="" href="/docs/configuration/expected-outputs/deterministic/#is-valid-openai-function-call"><code>is-valid-openai-tools-call</code></a> or <a class="" href="/docs/configuration/expected-outputs/deterministic/#is-valid-openai-tools-call"><code>is-valid-openai-tools-call</code></a> assertions to enforce an exact schema match between tools and the function definition.</p>
<p>To further test <code>tools</code> definitions, you can use the <code>javascript</code> assertion and/or <code>transform</code> directives. For example:</p>

style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token literal-property property" style="color:#36acaa">parameters</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token literal-property property" style="color:#36acaa">type</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;object&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token literal-property property" style="color:#36acaa">properties</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token literal-property property" style="color:#36acaa">unit</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">            </span><span class="token literal-property property" style="color:#36acaa">type</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;string&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line theme-code-block-highlighted-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">            </span><span class="token function-variable function" style="color:#d73a49">enum</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token parameter">vars</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=&gt;</span><span class="token plain"> vars</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">.</span><span class="token plain">units</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="using-functions">Using functions<a href="#using-functions" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Using functions" title="Direct link to Using functions" translate="no"></a></h3>
<blockquote>
<p><code>functions</code> and <code>function_call</code> is deprecated in favor of <code>tools</code> and <code>tool_choice</code>, see detail in <a href="https://platform.openai.com/docs/api-reference/chat/create#chat-create-function_call" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">OpenAI API reference</a>.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Use the <code>functions</code> config to define custom functions. Each function should be an object with a <code>name</code>, optional <code>description</code>, and <code>parameters</code>. For example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># yaml-language-server: $schema=https://promptfoo.dev/config-schema.json</span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;Get the current weather in a given location&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># ...</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Sometimes OpenAI function calls don&#x27;t match <code>functions</code> schemas. Use <a class="" href="/docs/configuration/expected-outputs/deterministic/#is-valid-openai-function-call"><code>is-valid-openai-function-call</code></a> assertions to enforce an exact schema match between function calls and the function definition.</p>
<p>To further test function call definitions, you can use the <code>javascript</code> assertion and/or <code>transform</code> directives. For example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tests</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">vars</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> is</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">valid</span><span plain">function</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">call</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token &#x27;get_current_weather&#x27;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> javascript</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> JSON.parse(output.arguments).location === &#x27;Boston</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"> MA&#x27;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">vars</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token <h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="loading-toolsfunctions-from-a-file">Loading tools/functions from a file<a href="#loading-toolsfunctions-from-a-file" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Loading tools/functions from a file" title="Direct link to Loading tools/functions from a file" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>Instead of duplicating function definitions across multiple configurations, you can reference an external YAML (or JSON) file that contains your functions. This allows you to maintain a single source of truth for your functions, which is particularly useful if you have multiple versions or regular changes to definitions.</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-tip admonition_WCGJ alert alert--success"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.5 0C3.48 0 1 2.19 1 5c0 .92.55 2.25 1 3 1.34 2.25 1.78 2.78 2 4v1h5v-1c.22-1.22.66-1.75 2-4 .45-.75 1-2.08 1-3 0-2.81-2.48-5-5.5-5zm3.64 7.48c-.25.44-.47.8-.67 1.11-.86 1.41-1.25 2.06-1.45 3.23-.02.05-.02.11-.02.17H5c0-.06 0-.13-.02-.17-.2-1.17-.59-1.83-1.45-3.23-.2-.31-.42-.67-.67-1.11C2.44 6.78 2 5.65 2 5c0-2.2 2.02-4 4.5-4 1.22 0 2.36.42 3.22 1.19C10.55 2.94 11 3.94 11 5c0 .66-.44 1.78-.86 2.48zM4 14h5c-.23 1.14-1.3 2-2.5 2s-2.27-.86-2.5-2z"></path></svg></span>tip</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>Tool definitions can be loaded from JSON, YAML, Python, or JavaScript files. For Python/JS files, specify a function name that returns the tool definitions: <code>file://tools.py:get_tools</code></p></div></div>
<p>To load your functions from a file, specify the file path in your provider configuration like so:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> file</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">//./path/to/provider_with_function.yaml</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>You can also use a pattern to load multiple files:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> file</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">//./path/to/provider_</span><span class="token important">*.yaml</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Here&#x27;s an example of how your <code>provider_with_function.yaml</code> might look:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">provider_with_function.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" <h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="using-response_format">Using <code>response_format</code><a href="#using-response_format" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to using-response_format" title="Direct link to using-response_format" translate="no"></a></h2>
<p>Promptfoo supports the <code>response_format</code> parameter, which allows you to specify the expected output format.</p>
<p><code>response_format</code> can be included in the provider config, or in the prompt config.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="prompt-config-example">Prompt config example<a href="#prompt-config-example" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Prompt config example" title="Direct link to Prompt config example" translate="no"></a></h4>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">prompts</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">label</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;Prompt #1&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">raw</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;You are a helpful math tutor. Solve {{problem}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">response_format</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> json_schema</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">json_schema</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">...</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="provider-config-example">Provider config example<a href="#provider-config-example" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Provider config example" title="Direct link to Provider config example" translate="no"></a></h4>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> openai</span><span class="token class="token plain"> json_schema</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">json_schema</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">...</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="external-file-references">External file references<a href="#external-file-references" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to External file references" title="Direct link to External file references" translate="no"></a></h4>
<p>To make it easier to manage large JSON schemas, external file references are supported for <code>response_format</code> in both Chat and Responses APIs. This is particularly useful for:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Reusing complex JSON schemas across multiple configurations</li>
<li class="">Managing large schemas in separate files for better organization</li>
<li class="">Version controlling schemas independently from configuration files</li>
</ul>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">response_format</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> file</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">//./path/to/response_format.json</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The external file should contain the complete <code>response_format</code> configuration object:</p>
<div class="language-json codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">response_format.json</div><div
