<p>For a complete example with the Chat API, see the <a href="https://github.com/promptfoo/promptfoo/tree/main/examples/openai-structured-output" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">OpenAI Structured Output example</a> or initialize it with:</p>
<div class="language-bash codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-bash codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">npx promptfoo@latest init </span><span class="token parameter variable" style="color:#36acaa">--example</span><span class="token plain"> openai-structured-output</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>For an example with the Responses API, see the <a href="https://github.com/promptfoo/promptfoo/tree/main/examples/openai-responses" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">OpenAI Responses API example</a> and run:</p>
<div class="language-bash codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-bash codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">npx promptfoo@latest init </span><span class="token parameter variable" style="color:#36acaa">--example</span><span class="token plain"> openai-responses</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token builtin class-name">cd</span><span class="token plain"> openai-responses</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">npx promptfoo@latest </span><span class="token builtin class-name">eval</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token parameter variable" style="color:#36acaa">-c</span><span class="token plain"> promptfooconfig.external-format.yaml</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="supported-environment-variables">Supported environment variables<a href="#supported-environment-variables" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Supported environment variables" title="Direct link to Supported environment variables" translate="no"></a></h2>
<p>These OpenAI-related environment variables are supported:</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>Variable</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>OPENAI_TEMPERATURE</code></td><td>Temperature model parameter, defaults to 0. Not supported by reasoning models.</td></tr><tr><td><code>OPENAI_MAX_TOKENS</code></td><td>Max_tokens model parameter, defaults to 1024. Not supported by reasoning models.</td></tr><tr><td><code>OPENAI_MAX_COMPLETION_TOKENS</code></td><td>Max_completion_tokens model parameter, defaults to 1024. Used by reasoning models.</td></tr><tr><td><code>OPENAI_REASONING_EFFORT</code></td><td>Reasoning effort parameter for reasoning models, defaults to &quot;medium&quot;. Options are &quot;low&quot;, &quot;medium&quot;, or &quot;high&quot;. Maps to <code>reasoning.effort</code> config parameter.</td></tr><tr><td><code>OPENAI_API_HOST</code></td><td>The hostname to use (useful if you&#x27;re using an API proxy). Takes priority over <code>OPENAI_BASE_URL</code>.</td></tr><tr><td><code>OPENAI_BASE_URL</code></td><td>The base URL (protocol + hostname + port) to use, this is a more general option than <code>OPENAI_API_HOST</code>.</td></tr><tr><td><code>OPENAI_API_KEY</code></td><td>OpenAI API key.</td></tr><tr><td><code>OPENAI_ORGANIZATION</code></td><td>The OpenAI organization key to use.</td></tr><tr><td><code>PROMPTFOO_DELAY_MS</code></td><td>Number of milliseconds to delay between API calls. Useful if you are hitting OpenAI rate limits (defaults to 0).</td></tr><tr><td><code>PROMPTFOO_REQUEST_BACKOFF_MS</code></td><td>Base number of milliseconds to backoff and retry if a request fails (defaults to 5000).</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="evaluating-assistants">Evaluating assistants<a href="#evaluating-assistants" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Evaluating assistants" title="Direct link to Evaluating assistants" translate="no"></a></h2>
<p>To test out an Assistant via OpenAI&#x27;s Assistants API, first create an Assistant in the <a href="https://platform.openai.com/playground" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">API playground</a>.</p>
<p>Set functions, code interpreter, and files for retrieval as necessary.</p>
<p>Then, include the assistant in your config:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">prompts</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;Write a tweet about {{topic}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> openai</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">assistant</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">asst_fEhNN3MClMamLfKLkIaoIpgZ</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tests</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">vars</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">topic</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bananas</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># ...</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Code interpreter, function calls, and retrievals will be included in the output alongside chat messages. Note that the evaluator creates a new thread for each eval.</p>
<p>The following properties can be overwritten in provider config:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>model</code> - OpenAI model to use</li>
<li class=""><code>instructions</code> - System prompt</li>
<li class=""><code>tools</code> - Enabled <a href="https://platform.openai.com/docs/api-reference/runs/createRun" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">tools</a></li>
<li class=""><code>thread.messages</code> - A list of message objects that the thread is created with.</li>
<li class=""><code>temperature</code> - Temperature for the model</li>
<li class=""><code>toolChoice</code> - Controls whether the AI should use a tool</li>
<li class=""><code>tool_resources</code> - Tool resources to include in the thread - see <a href="https://platform.openai.com/docs/assistants/migration" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Assistant v2 tool resources</a></li>
<li class=""><code>attachments</code> - File attachments to include in messages - see <a href="https://platform.openai.com/docs/assistants/migration" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Assistant v2 attachments</a></li>
</ul>
<p>Here&#x27;s an example of a more detailed config:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span <h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="automatically-handling-function-tool-calls">Automatically handling function tool calls<a href="#automatically-handling-function-tool-calls" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Automatically handling function tool calls" title="Direct link to Automatically handling function tool calls" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>You can specify JavaScript callbacks that are automatically called to create
the output of a function tool call.</p>
<p>This requires defining your config in a JavaScript file instead of YAML.</p>
<div class="language-js codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-js codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">module</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">.</span><span class="token plain">exports </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">/** @type {import(&#x27;promptfoo&#x27;).TestSuiteConfig} */</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token literal-property property" style="color:#36acaa">prompts</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;Please add the following numbers together: {{a}} and {{b}}&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token literal-property property" style="color:#36acaa">providers</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token literal-property style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;openai:assistant:asst_fEhNN3MClMamLfKLkIaoIpgZ&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token literal-property property" style="color:#36acaa">tools</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span <h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="audio-capabilities">Audio capabilities<a href="#audio-capabilities" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Audio capabilities" title="Direct link to Audio capabilities" translate="no"></a></h2>
<p>OpenAI models with audio support (like <code>gpt-audio</code>, <code>gpt-audio-mini</code>, <code>gpt-4o-audio-preview</code> and <code>gpt-4o-mini-audio-preview</code>) can process audio inputs and generate audio outputs. This enables testing speech-to-text, text-to-speech, and speech-to-speech capabilities.</p>
<p><strong>Available audio models:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>gpt-audio</code> - Latest audio model ($2.50/$10 per 1M text tokens, $40/$80 per 1M audio tokens)</li>
<li class=""><code>gpt-audio-mini</code> - Cost-efficient audio model ($0.60/$2.40 per 1M text tokens, $10/$20 per 1M audio tokens)</li>
<li class=""><code>gpt-4o-audio-preview</code> - Preview audio model</li>
<li class=""><code>gpt-4o-mini-audio-preview</code> - Preview mini audio model</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="using-audio-inputs">Using audio inputs<a href="#using-audio-inputs" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Using audio inputs" title="Direct link to Using audio inputs" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>You can include audio files in your prompts using the following format:</p>
<div class="language-json codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">audio-input.json</div><div <p>With a corresponding configuration:</p>

issue</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Supported audio file formats include WAV, MP3, OGG, AAC, M4A, and FLAC.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="audio-configuration-options">Audio configuration options<a href="#audio-configuration-options" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Audio configuration options" title="Direct link to Audio configuration options" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>The audio configuration supports these parameters:</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th><th>Default</th><th>Options</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>voice</code></td><td>Voice for audio generation</td><td>alloy</td><td>alloy, echo, fable, onyx, nova, shimmer</td></tr><tr><td><code>format</code></td><td>Audio format to generate</td><td>wav</td><td>wav, mp3, opus, aac</td></tr><tr><td><code>speed</code></td><td>Speaking speed multiplier</td><td>1.0</td><td>Any number between 0.25 and 4.0</td></tr><tr><td><code>bitrate</code></td><td>Bitrate for compressed formats</td><td>-</td><td>e.g., &quot;128k&quot;, &quot;256k&quot;</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>In the web UI, audio outputs display with an embedded player and transcript. For a complete working example, see the <a href="https://github.com/promptfoo/promptfoo/tree/main/examples/openai-audio" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">OpenAI audio example</a> or initialize it with:</p>
<div class="language-bash codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-bash codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">npx promptfoo@latest init </span><span class="token parameter variable" style="color:#36acaa">--example</span><span class="token plain"> openai-audio</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="audio-transcription">Audio transcription<a href="#audio-transcription" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Audio transcription" title="Direct link to Audio transcription" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>OpenAI provides dedicated transcription models for converting speech to text. These models charge per minute of audio rather than per token.</p>
<p><strong>Available transcription models:</strong></p>
<table><thead><tr><th>Model</th><th>Description</th><th>Cost per minute</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>whisper-1</code></td><td>Original Whisper transcription model</td><td>$0.006</td></tr><tr><td><code>gpt-4o-transcribe</code></td><td>GPT-4o optimized for transcription</td><td>$0.006</td></tr><tr><td><code>gpt-4o-mini-transcribe</code></td><td>Faster, more cost-effective option</td><td>$0.003</td></tr><tr><td><code>gpt-4o-transcribe-diarize</code></td><td>Identifies different speakers</td><td>$0.006</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>To use transcription models, specify the provider format <code>openai:transcription:&lt;model name&gt;</code>:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div <h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="transcription-configuration-options">Transcription configuration options<a href="#transcription-configuration-options" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Transcription configuration options" title="Direct link to Transcription configuration options" translate="no"></a></h4>
<table><thead><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th><th>Options</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>language</code></td><td>Language of the audio (ISO-639-1)</td><td>e.g., &#x27;en&#x27;, &#x27;es&#x27;, &#x27;fr&#x27;</td></tr><tr><td><code>prompt</code></td><td>Context to improve transcription accuracy</td><td>Any text string</td></tr><tr><td><code>temperature</code></td><td>Controls randomness (0-1)</td><td>Number between 0 and 1</td></tr><tr><td><code>timestamp_granularities</code></td><td>Get word or segment-level timestamps</td><td>[&#x27;word&#x27;, &#x27;segment&#x27;]</td></tr><tr><td><code>num_speakers</code></td><td>Expected number of speakers (diarization)</td><td>Number</td></tr><tr><td><code>speaker_labels</code></td><td>Names for speakers (diarization)</td><td>Array of strings</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>Supported audio formats include MP3, MP4, MPEG, MPGA, M4A, WAV, and WEBM.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="diarization-example">Diarization example<a href="#diarization-example" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Diarization example" title="Direct link to Diarization example" translate="no"></a></h4>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="realtime-api-models">Realtime API Models<a href="#realtime-api-models" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Realtime API Models" title="Direct link to Realtime API Models" translate="no"></a></h2>
<p>The Realtime API allows for real-time communication with GPT-4o class models using WebSockets, supporting both text and audio inputs/outputs with streaming responses.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="supported-realtime-models">Supported Realtime Models<a href="#supported-realtime-models" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Supported Realtime Models" title="Direct link to Supported Realtime Models" translate="no"></a></h3>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>gpt-realtime</code> - Latest realtime model ($4/$16 per 1M text tokens, $40/$80 per 1M audio tokens)</li>
<li class=""><code>gpt-realtime-mini</code> - Cost-efficient realtime model ($0.60/$2.40 per 1M text tokens, $10/$20 per 1M audio tokens)</li>
<li class=""><code>gpt-4o-realtime-preview-2024-12-17</code></li>
<li class=""><code>gpt-5-mini-realtime-preview-2024-12-17</code></li>
</ul>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="using-realtime-api">Using Realtime API<a href="#using-realtime-api" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Using Realtime API" title="Direct link to Using Realtime API" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>To use the OpenAI Realtime API, use the provider format <code>openai:realtime:&lt;model name&gt;</code>:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> openai</span><span class="token atrule" style="color:#00a4db">instructions</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;You are a helpful assistant.&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">temperature</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.7</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">websocketTimeout</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">60000</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># 60 seconds</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Optional: point to custom/proxy endpoints; WS URL is derived automatically</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span <h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="realtime-specific-configuration-options">Realtime-specific Configuration Options<a href="#realtime-specific-configuration-options" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Realtime-specific Configuration Options" title="Direct link to Realtime-specific Configuration Options" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>The Realtime API configuration supports these parameters in addition to standard OpenAI parameters:</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th><th>Default</th><th>Options</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>modalities</code></td><td>Types of content the model can process and generate</td><td>[&#x27;text&#x27;, &#x27;audio&#x27;]</td><td>&#x27;text&#x27;, &#x27;audio&#x27;</td></tr><tr><td><code>voice</code></td><td>Voice for audio generation</td><td>&#x27;alloy&#x27;</td><td>alloy, echo, fable, onyx, nova, shimmer</td></tr><tr><td><code>instructions</code></td><td>System instructions for the model</td><td>&#x27;You are a helpful...&#x27;</td><td>Any text string</td></tr><tr><td><code>input_audio_format</code></td><td>Format of audio input</td><td>&#x27;pcm16&#x27;</td><td>&#x27;pcm16&#x27;, &#x27;g711_ulaw&#x27;, &#x27;g711_alaw&#x27;</td></tr><tr><td><code>output_audio_format</code></td><td>Format of audio output</td><td>&#x27;pcm16&#x27;</td><td>&#x27;pcm16&#x27;, &#x27;g711_ulaw&#x27;, &#x27;g711_alaw&#x27;</td></tr><tr><td><code>websocketTimeout</code></td><td>Timeout for WebSocket connection (milliseconds)</td><td>30000</td><td>Any number</td></tr><tr><td><code>max_response_output_tokens</code></td><td>Maximum tokens in model response</td><td>&#x27;inf&#x27;</td><td>Number or &#x27;inf&#x27;</td></tr><tr><td><code>tools</code></td><td>Array of tool definitions for function calling</td><td>[]</td><td>Array of tool objects</td></tr><tr><td><code>tool_choice</code></td><td>Controls how tools are selected</td><td>&#x27;auto&#x27;</td><td>&#x27;none&#x27;, &#x27;auto&#x27;, &#x27;required&#x27;, or object</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="custom-endpoints-and-proxies-realtime">Custom endpoints and proxies (Realtime)<a href="#custom-endpoints-and-proxies-realtime" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Custom endpoints and proxies (Realtime)" title="Direct link to Custom endpoints and proxies (Realtime)" translate="no"></a></h4>
<p>The Realtime provider respects the same base URL configuration as other OpenAI providers. The WebSocket URL is derived from <code>getApiUrl()</code> by converting protocols: <code>https://</code>  <code>wss://</code> and <code>http://</code>  <code>ws://</code>.</p>
<p>You can use this to target Azure-compatible endpoints, proxies, or local/dev servers:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> openai</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">realtime</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">gpt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">4o</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">realtime</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">preview</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">apiBaseUrl</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://my-custom-api.com/v1&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># connects to wss://my-custom-api.com/v1/realtime</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">modalities</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;text&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">temperature</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.7</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Environment variables <code>OPENAI_API_BASE_URL</code> and <code>OPENAI_BASE_URL</code> also apply to Realtime WebSocket connections.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="function-calling-with-realtime-api">Function Calling with Realtime API<a href="#function-calling-with-realtime-api" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Function Calling with Realtime API" title="Direct link to Function Calling with Realtime API" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>The Realtime API supports function calling via tools, similar to the Chat API. Here&#x27;s an example configuration:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span <h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="complete-example">Complete Example<a href="#complete-example" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Complete Example" title="Direct link to Complete Example" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>For a complete working example that demonstrates the Realtime API capabilities, see the <a href="https://github.com/promptfoo/promptfoo/tree/main/examples/openai-realtime" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">OpenAI Realtime API example</a> or initialize it with:</p>
<div class="language-bash codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-bash codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">npx promptfoo@latest init </span><span class="token parameter variable" style="color:#36acaa">--example</span><span class="token plain"> openai-realtime</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>This example includes:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Basic single-turn interactions with the Realtime API</li>
<li class="">Multi-turn conversations with persistent context</li>
<li class="">Conversation threading with separate conversation IDs</li>
<li class="">JavaScript prompt function for properly formatting messages</li>
<li class="">Function calling with the Realtime API</li>
<li class="">Detailed documentation on handling content types correctly</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="input-and-message-format">Input and Message Format<a href="#input-and-message-format" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Input and Message Format" title="Direct link to Input and Message Format" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>When using the Realtime API with promptfoo, you can specify the prompt in JSON format:</p>
<div class="language-json codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">realtime-input.json</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-json codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;user&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span       </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;type&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The Realtime API supports the same multimedia formats as the Chat API, allowing you to include images and audio in your prompts.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="multi-turn-conversations">Multi-Turn Conversations<a href="#multi-turn-conversations" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Multi-Turn Conversations" title="Direct link to Multi-Turn Conversations" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>The Realtime API supports multi-turn conversations with persistent context. For implementation details and examples, see the <a href="https://github.com/promptfoo/promptfoo/tree/main/examples/openai-realtime" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">OpenAI Realtime example</a>, which demonstrates both single-turn interactions and conversation threading using the <code>conversationId</code> metadata property.</p>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>Important</strong>: When implementing multi-turn conversations, use <code>type: &quot;input_text&quot;</code> for user inputs and <code>type: &quot;text&quot;</code> for assistant responses.</p>
</blockquote>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="responses-api">Responses API<a href="#responses-api" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Responses API" title="Direct link to Responses API" translate="no"></a></h2>
<p>OpenAI&#x27;s Responses API is the most advanced interface for generating model responses, supporting text and image inputs, function calling, and conversation state. It provides access to OpenAI&#x27;s full suite of features including reasoning models like o1, o3, and o4 series.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="supported-responses-models">Supported Responses Models<a href="#supported-responses-models" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Supported Responses Models" title="Direct link to Supported Responses Models" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>The Responses API supports a wide range of models, including:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>gpt-5</code> - OpenAI&#x27;s most capable vision model</li>
<li class=""><code>o1</code> - Powerful reasoning model</li>
<li class=""><code>o1-mini</code> - Smaller, more affordable reasoning model</li>
<li class=""><code>o1-pro</code> - Enhanced reasoning model with more compute</li>
<li class=""><code>o3-pro</code> - Highest-tier reasoning model</li>
<li class=""><code>o3</code> - OpenAI&#x27;s most powerful reasoning model</li>
<li class=""><code>o3-mini</code> - Smaller, more affordable reasoning model</li>
<li class=""><code>o4-mini</code> - Latest fast, cost-effective reasoning model</li>
<li class=""><code>codex-mini-latest</code> - Fast reasoning model optimized for the Codex CLI</li>
<li class=""><code>gpt-5-codex</code> - GPT-5 based coding model optimized for code generation</li>
<li class=""><code>gpt-5-pro</code> - Premium GPT-5 model with highest reasoning capability ($15/$120 per 1M tokens)</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="using-the-responses-api">Using the Responses API<a href="#using-the-responses-api" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Using the Responses API" title="Direct link to Using the Responses API" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>To use the OpenAI Responses API, use the provider format <code>openai:responses:&lt;model name&gt;</code>:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> openai</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">responses</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">gpt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">5</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">temperature</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.7</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_output_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">500</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">instructions</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;You are a helpful, creative AI assistant.&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="responses-specific-configuration-options">Responses-specific Configuration Options<a href="#responses-specific-configuration-options" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Responses-specific Configuration Options" title="Direct link to Responses-specific Configuration Options" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>The Responses API configuration supports these parameters in addition to standard OpenAI parameters:</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th><th>Default</th><th>Options</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>instructions</code></td><td>System instructions for the model</td><td>None</td><td>Any text string</td></tr><tr><td><code>max_output_tokens</code></td><td>Maximum tokens to generate in the response</td><td>1024</td><td>Any number</td></tr><tr><td><code>metadata</code></td><td>Key-value pairs attached to the model response</td><td>None</td><td>Map of string keys to string values</td></tr><tr><td><code>parallel_tool_calls</code></td><td>Allow model to run tool calls in parallel</td><td>true</td><td>Boolean</td></tr><tr><td><code>previous_response_id</code></td><td>ID of a previous response for multi-turn context</td><td>None</td><td>String</td></tr><tr><td><code>store</code></td><td>Whether to store the response for later retrieval</td><td>true</td><td>Boolean</td></tr><tr><td><code>truncation</code></td><td>Strategy to handle context window overflow</td><td>&#x27;disabled&#x27;</td><td>&#x27;auto&#x27;, &#x27;disabled&#x27;</td></tr><tr><td><code>reasoning</code></td><td>Configuration for reasoning models</td><td>None</td><td>Object with <code>effort</code> field</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="mcp-model-context-protocol-support">MCP (Model Context Protocol) Support<a href="#mcp-model-context-protocol-support" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to MCP (Model Context Protocol) Support" title="Direct link to MCP (Model Context Protocol) Support" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>The Responses API supports OpenAI&#x27;s MCP integration, allowing models to use remote MCP servers to perform tasks. MCP tools enable access to external services and APIs through a standardized protocol.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="basic-mcp-configuration">Basic MCP Configuration<a href="#basic-mcp-configuration" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Basic MCP Configuration" title="Direct link to Basic MCP Configuration" translate="no"></a></h4>
<p>To use MCP tools with the Responses API, add them to the <code>tools</code> array:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token <h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="mcp-tool-configuration-options">MCP Tool Configuration Options<a href="#mcp-tool-configuration-options" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to MCP Tool Configuration Options" title="Direct link to MCP Tool Configuration Options" translate="no"></a></h4>
<table><thead><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th><th>Required</th><th>Options</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>type</code></td><td>Tool type (must be &#x27;mcp&#x27;)</td><td>Yes</td><td>&#x27;mcp&#x27;</td></tr><tr><td><code>server_label</code></td><td>Label to identify the MCP server</td><td>Yes</td><td>Any string</td></tr><tr><td><code>server_url</code></td><td>URL of the remote MCP server</td><td>Yes</td><td>Valid URL</td></tr><tr><td><code>require_approval</code></td><td>Approval settings for tool calls</td><td>No</td><td>&#x27;never&#x27; or object with approval settings</td></tr><tr><td><code>allowed_tools</code></td><td>Specific tools to allow from the server</td><td>No</td><td>Array of tool names</td></tr><tr><td><code>headers</code></td><td>Custom headers for authentication</td><td>No</td><td>Object with header key-value pairs</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="authentication-with-mcp-servers">Authentication with MCP Servers<a href="#authentication-with-mcp-servers" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Authentication with MCP Servers" title="Direct link to Authentication with MCP Servers" translate="no"></a></h4>
<p>Most MCP servers require authentication. Use the <code>headers</code> parameter to provide API keys or tokens:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div <h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="filtering-mcp-tools">Filtering MCP Tools<a href="#filtering-mcp-tools" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Filtering MCP Tools" title="Direct link to Filtering MCP Tools" translate="no"></a></h4>

style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> contains</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;transport protocols&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>For a complete working example, see the <a href="https://github.com/promptfoo/promptfoo/tree/main/examples/openai-mcp" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">OpenAI MCP example</a> or initialize it with:</p>
<div class="language-bash codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-bash codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">npx promptfoo@latest init </span><span class="token parameter variable" style="color:#36acaa">--example</span><span class="token plain"> openai-mcp</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="reasoning-models">Reasoning Models<a href="#reasoning-models" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Reasoning Models" title="Direct link to Reasoning Models" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>When using reasoning models like <code>o1</code>, <code>o1-pro</code>, <code>o3</code>, <code>o3-pro</code>, <code>o3-mini</code>, or <code>o4-mini</code>, you can control the reasoning effort:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> openai</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">responses</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">o3</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">reasoning</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">effort</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;medium&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Can be &quot;low&quot;, &quot;medium&quot;, or &quot;high&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_output_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">1000</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Reasoning models &quot;think before they answer,&quot; generating internal reasoning that isn&#x27;t visible in the output but counts toward token usage and billing.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="o3-and-o4-mini-models">o3 and o4-mini Models<a href="#o3-and-o4-mini-models" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to o3 and o4-mini Models" title="Direct link to o3 and o4-mini Models" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>OpenAI offers advanced reasoning models in the o-series:</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="o3-and-o4-mini">o3 and o4-mini<a href="#o3-and-o4-mini" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to o3 and o4-mini" title="Direct link to o3 and o4-mini" translate="no"></a></h4>
<p>These reasoning models provide different performance and efficiency profiles:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>o3</strong>: Powerful reasoning model, optimized for complex mathematical, scientific, and coding tasks</li>
<li class=""><strong>o4-mini</strong>: Efficient reasoning model with strong performance in coding and visual tasks at lower cost</li>
</ul>
<p>Both models feature:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Large context window (200,000 tokens)</li>
<li class="">High maximum output tokens (100,000 tokens)</li>
</ul>
<p>For current specifications and pricing information, refer to <a href="https://openai.com/pricing" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">OpenAI&#x27;s pricing page</a>.</p>
<p>Example configuration:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;high&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_output_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> openai</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">responses</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">o4</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">mini</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;medium&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_output_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">1000</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="deep-research-models-responses-api-only">Deep Research Models (Responses API Only)<a href="#deep-research-models-responses-api-only" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Deep Research Models (Responses API Only)" title="Direct link to Deep Research Models (Responses API Only)" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>Deep research models (<code>o3-deep-research</code>, <code>o4-mini-deep-research</code>) are specialized reasoning models designed for complex research tasks that require web search capabilities.</p>
<p>Available models:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>o3-deep-research</code> - Most powerful deep research model ($10/1M input, $40/1M output)</li>
<li class=""><code>o3-deep-research-2025-06-26</code> - Snapshot version</li>
<li class=""><code>o4-mini-deep-research</code> - Faster, more affordable ($2/1M input, $8/1M output)</li>
<li class=""><code>o4-mini-deep-research-2025-06-26</code> - Snapshot version</li>
</ul>
<p>All deep research models:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Require</strong> <code>web_search_preview</code> tool to be configured</li>
<li class="">Support 200,000 token context window</li>
<li class="">Support up to 100,000 output tokens</li>
<li class="">May take 2-10 minutes to complete research tasks</li>
<li class="">Use significant tokens for reasoning before generating output</li>
</ul>
<p>Example configuration:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">promptfooconfig.yaml</div><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span <h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="response-format">Response Format<a href="#response-format" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Response Format" title="Direct link to Response Format" translate="no"></a></h4>
<p>Deep research models return specialized output items:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>web_search_call</strong>: Web search actions (search, open_page, find_in_page)</li>
<li class=""><strong>code_interpreter_call</strong>: Code execution for analysis</li>
<li class=""><strong>message</strong>: Final answer with inline citations and annotations</li>
</ul>
<p>Example response structure:</p>
<div class="language-json codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-json codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;output&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;type&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;web_search_call&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;action&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;type&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;search&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;query&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;latest AI research papers 2025&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;type&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;message&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;type&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;output_text&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token property" class="token plain">          </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;annotations&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">            </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">              </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;url&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;Paper Title&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">              </span><span class="token property" class="token plain">              </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;end_index&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">145</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">            </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="best-practices-2">Best Practices<a href="#best-practices-2" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Best Practices" title="Direct link to Best Practices" translate="no"></a></h4>
<ol>
<li class=""><strong>Use Background Mode</strong>: For production, always use <code>background: true</code> to handle long response times</li>
<li class=""><strong>Set High Token Limits</strong>: Use <code>max_output_tokens: 50000</code> or higher</li>
<li class=""><strong>Configure Timeouts</strong>: Set <code>PROMPTFOO_EVAL_TIMEOUT_MS=600000</code> for 10-minute timeouts</li>
<li class=""><strong>Control Costs</strong>: Use <code>max_tool_calls</code> to limit the number of searches</li>
<li class=""><strong>Enhance Prompts</strong>: Consider using a faster model to clarify/rewrite prompts before deep research</li>
</ol>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="timeout-configuration">Timeout Configuration<a href="#timeout-configuration" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Timeout Configuration" title="Direct link to Timeout Configuration" translate="no"></a></h4>
<p>Deep research models automatically use appropriate timeouts:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">If <code>PROMPTFOO_EVAL_TIMEOUT_MS</code> is set, it will be used for the API call</li>
<li class="">Otherwise, deep research models default to a 10-minute timeout (600,000ms)</li>
<li class="">Regular models continue to use the standard 5-minute timeout</li>
</ul>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-bash codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-bash codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Set a custom timeout for all evaluations</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token builtin class-name">export</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token assign-left variable" style="color:#36acaa">PROMPTFOO_EVAL_TIMEOUT_MS</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">900000</span><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># 15 minutes</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Or set the default API timeout (affects all providers)</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token builtin class-name">export</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token assign-left variable" style="color:#36acaa">REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">600000</span><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># 10 minutes</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-tip admonition_WCGJ alert alert--success"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.5 0C3.48 0 1 2.19 1 5c0 .92.55 2.25 1 3 1.34 2.25 1.78 2.78 2 4v1h5v-1c.22-1.22.66-1.75 2-4 .45-.75 1-2.08 1-3 0-2.81-2.48-5-5.5-5zm3.64 7.48c-.25.44-.47.8-.67 1.11-.86 1.41-1.25 2.06-1.45 3.23-.02.05-.02.11-.02.17H5c0-.06 0-.13-.02-.17-.2-1.17-.59-1.83-1.45-3.23-.2-.31-.42-.67-.67-1.11C2.44 6.78 2 5.65 2 5c0-2.2 2.02-4 4.5-4 1.22 0 2.36.42 3.22 1.19C10.55 2.94 11 3.94 11 5c0 .66-.44 1.78-.86 2.48zM4 14h5c-.23 1.14-1.3 2-2.5 2s-2.27-.86-2.5-2z"></path></svg></span>tip</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>Deep research models require high <code>max_output_tokens</code> values (50,000+) and long timeouts. Set <code>PROMPTFOO_EVAL_TIMEOUT_MS=600000</code> for 10-minute timeouts.</p></div></div>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-warning admonition_WCGJ alert alert--warning"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8.893 1.5c-.183-.31-.52-.5-.887-.5s-.703.19-.886.5L.138 13.499a.98.98 0 0 0 0 1.001c.193.31.53.501.886.501h13.964c.367 0 .704-.19.877-.5a1.03 1.03 0 0 0 .01-1.002L8.893 1.5zm.133 11.497H6.987v-2.003h2.039v2.003zm0-3.004H6.987V5.987h2.039v4.006z"></path></svg></span>warning</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>The <code>web_search_preview</code> tool is <strong>required</strong> for deep research models. The provider will return an error if this tool is not configured.</p></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="gpt-5-pro-timeout-configuration">GPT-5-pro Timeout Configuration<a href="#gpt-5-pro-timeout-configuration" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to GPT-5-pro Timeout Configuration" title="Direct link to GPT-5-pro Timeout Configuration" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>GPT-5-pro is a long-running model that often requires extended timeouts due to its advanced reasoning capabilities. Like deep research models, GPT-5-pro <strong>automatically</strong> receives a 10-minute timeout (600,000ms) instead of the standard 5-minute timeout.</p>
<p><strong>Automatic timeout behavior:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="">GPT-5-pro automatically gets a 10-minute timeout (600,000ms) - <strong>no configuration needed</strong></li>
<li class="">If you need longer, set <code>PROMPTFOO_EVAL_TIMEOUT_MS</code> (e.g., 900000 for 15 minutes)</li>
<li class=""><code>REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS</code> is <strong>ignored</strong> for GPT-5-pro (the automatic timeout takes precedence)</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Most users won&#x27;t need any timeout configuration</strong> - the automatic 10-minute timeout is sufficient for most GPT-5-pro requests.</p>
<p><strong>If you experience timeouts, configure this:</strong></p>
<div class="language-bash codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-bash codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Only if you need more than the automatic 10 minutes</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token builtin class-name">export</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token assign-left variable" style="color:#36acaa">PROMPTFOO_EVAL_TIMEOUT_MS</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">1200000</span><span class="token plain">   </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># 20 minutes</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># For infrastructure reliability (recommended)</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token builtin class-name">export</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token assign-left variable" style="color:#36acaa">PROMPTFOO_RETRY_5XX</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token plain">true            </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Retry 502 Bad Gateway errors</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token builtin class-name">export</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token assign-left variable" style="color:#36acaa">PROMPTFOO_REQUEST_BACKOFF_MS</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">10000</span><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Longer retry backoff</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Reduce concurrency to avoid rate limits</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">promptfoo </span><span class="token builtin class-name">eval</span><span class="token plain"> --max-concurrency </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">2</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p><strong>Common GPT-5-pro errors and solutions:</strong></p>
<p>If you encounter errors with GPT-5-pro:</p>
<ol>
<li class=""><strong>Request timed out</strong> - If GPT-5-pro needs more than the automatic 10 minutes, set <code>PROMPTFOO_EVAL_TIMEOUT_MS=1200000</code> (20 minutes)</li>
<li class=""><strong>502 Bad Gateway</strong> - Enable <code>PROMPTFOO_RETRY_5XX=true</code> to retry Cloudflare/OpenAI infrastructure timeouts</li>
<li class=""><strong>getaddrinfo ENOTFOUND</strong> - Transient DNS errors; reduce concurrency with <code>--max-concurrency 2</code></li>
<li class=""><strong>Upstream connection errors</strong> - OpenAI load balancer issues; increase backoff with <code>PROMPTFOO_REQUEST_BACKOFF_MS=10000</code></li>
</ol>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-tip admonition_WCGJ alert alert--success"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.5 0C3.48 0 1 2.19 1 5c0 .92.55 2.25 1 3 1.34 2.25 1.78 2.78 2 4v1h5v-1c.22-1.22.66-1.75 2-4 .45-.75 1-2.08 1-3 0-2.81-2.48-5-5.5-5zm3.64 7.48c-.25.44-.47.8-.67 1.11-.86 1.41-1.25 2.06-1.45 3.23-.02.05-.02.11-.02.17H5c0-.06 0-.13-.02-.17-.2-1.17-.59-1.83-1.45-3.23-.2-.31-.42-.67-.67-1.11C2.44 6.78 2 5.65 2 5c0-2.2 2.02-4 4.5-4 1.22 0 2.36.42 3.22 1.19C10.55 2.94 11 3.94 11 5c0 .66-.44 1.78-.86 2.48zM4 14h5c-.23 1.14-1.3 2-2.5 2s-2.27-.86-2.5-2z"></path></svg></span>tip</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>GPT-5-pro automatically gets a 10-minute timeout - you likely don&#x27;t need any timeout configuration. If you see infrastructure errors (502, DNS failures), enable <code>PROMPTFOO_RETRY_5XX=true</code> and reduce concurrency.</p></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="sending-images-in-prompts-1">Sending Images in Prompts<a href="#sending-images-in-prompts-1" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Sending Images in Prompts" title="Direct link to Sending Images in Prompts" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>The Responses API supports structured prompts with text and image inputs. Example:</p>
<div class="language-json codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockTitle_kY6l">prompt.json</div><div
